<user_id>107080937679323728846</user_id></record></dataset><record>
<pictures>None</pictures>< username>
Anastasia E< /username>
<Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
Came in 4 days ago for 2 lower wisdom tooth extractions.

**I've had 4 secondary molars extracted at once by a previous dentist a few years back and it was the most traumatic experience (I felt everything, they wouldn't listen, my mouth was cut open everywhere...sides of cheeks, roof of mouth, lips, etc). **

I was nervous to say the least about my wisdom teeth and insisted they put me under anesthetic . They accommodated my request with no issue or questions and got me scheduled quickly.

The procedure was extremely quick (from being put under , to waking up) couldn't have been more than an hour. Dr. Mashhadian had decided only one needed to be extracted while I was under anesthesia. That the second wisdom tooth wasn't the issue on my left, another tooth was responsible for the pain on that side. The staff explained everything to my boyfriend to follow up with me after anesthesia wore off.

My prescriptions were filled immediately,  the staff (Ruth and I believe Crystal?) have been nothing but kind and prompt in answering my silly follow up questions . The sutures are short enough to cause no extra irritation,  the extraction site seems to be healing quickly,  and overall my procedure / experience with Desert Dental couldn't have gone smoother.   Thank you to Desert Dental and their staff!

< review>
We've used Caccia Plumbing several times in the past. They are prompt in returning our call and in scheduling appointments. They sent a picture of    Joe Sullivan, the plumber, who we would expect to come that day.
Joe was on time and very mindful about safety protocols because of the pandemic. He was ready with his own shoe covers which I had required of anyone doing work inside the house.
He diagnosed what was causing several problems we described with the kitchen faucet, the hot water supply, and the main valve that controls the water supply to the house. He also explained how he would fix them, for how long, and for how much.
He worked efficiently and answered any questions we had during the process. He kept the area neatly cleaned up after he was done.
Joe is a pro at what he does and an asset to the Caccia team.</review>

<Rating>5< /Rating><text>After a minor reschedule, Joe Sullivan was sent out to repair a leak in my kitchen sink drain. Joe listened attentively to my explanation of the history of the relocation of the drain and the problems it caused. < text>
We recently had some plumbing problems requiring a new line from the house to the street. As part of the work, we thought it would be a good idea to look under the house as well, as the pipes are old. That is where Caccia Plumbing comes in.
We had an excellent experience with first the inspection of the pipes and recommendations on the work needed. We then received a very detailed and quick plan of action and a quote for the work.
Of course we looked at other companies but chose Caccia for their professionalism and responsiveness.
Today, Andrei showed up within 15 minutes of the quoted time by the dispatcher. He came with a clean uniform, greeted me and reviewed the work. He even helped me move some of the items in the shed to get better access to the door leading to the crawl space. He was professional, & took the time to make sure that some items left in the shed were covered so they would not be in harms way.
The work began and we interacted several times during the work to test joints and pipes with water etc. Each time he was quite courteous. And and at the end, he cleaned up, knocked on the door, and apologized for getting a little mark on an item in the shed! He showed me pictures of his work and items corrected as well as an overall movie of the area, and reported that the work was timely as there was moisture in and around the concrete, indicating a small leak. We will be getting these for our records with a final report.
All in all, my wife and I are really impressed and would recommend highly this service for anyone needing some plumbing work. I know I can sleep now with the knowledge that we will not be having any troubles for quite some time.< /text>

< Text>
We had a number of plumbing issues: leaky sinks, weak pressure in shower heads, a broken kitchen sink and disposal unit. We were told by numerous plumbers in the past that the kitchen sink disposal unit could not be fixed due to the angle of the piping behind the custom cabinetry. A fix would require breaking through the cabinetry.

Joseph Stevenson worked on the main kitchen sink and disposal unit. He was able to do what prior plumbers said could not be done. He worked in a tight space behind the cabinets by only breaking through the back wall and leaving everything else in tact. Once he got everything working, he replaced the back wall of the cabinet and cleaned everything to leave no trace of the work. Amazing!

While Caccia runs a bit more expensive than other plumbing companies, our experience was exceptional, and we thought we got what we paid for. < Review>
We have a very bad experience with this company.  When we asked for an estimate for our kitchen pipe leaking problem, we were told it was free.  After Nate came to our house, he went into the crawl space, then he immediately came right back out and said it was a mess in the crawl space, he advised us to hire a professional restoration company to clean it up first before he can see the pipe problem.  Therefore, he can not give us an estimate.  He said his service for that date was $197.00.   Then we received a charge bill from our credit company that he actually charged us $425.00.    We called the company and talked to the manager, he then sent us a refund check for $140.00.  So, we ended up paying $285 for their half hour service and did not even have an estimate.
We called another company to do the same estimate the next day and the one hour work with a real written estimate was only cost us $49.00.
I suggest all customer to be very careful to do business with this company.  Found out all the hidden cost before you have them do the job for you.     We spent $285.00 for  a lesson learnt.<//Review>

< text>
Had Caccia come over to fix a leaky shower faucet this morning and it was incredibly smooth and seamless. We called two days earlier in the week and scheduled them to come by between 8-9am. Ofa arrived at almost exactly 8:30.

He came in and I showed him the problem with the shower. We then walked around to shutoff the water and take a look at our water heater. He was super informative the entire time and made sure to take the time to help me understand what exactly he was looking at and why.

He then spent some time replacing the parts in the faucet that needed fixing and went over each step.

Ofa was in and out  with all the fixes in place and had a happy customer in a little over an hour.

I highly recommend Caccia Plumbing and would ask to have Ofa be the technician. He was super professional and courteous.</text>
